# Site name:      Moon Lake
# Place:          USA:North Dakota

# Longitude:      98.09.30W      ( -98.158333)
# Elevation(m):   444
# Sigle:          MOONLAKE
# Entity name:
# Contact person: Grimm, E.C.
# Entity notes:   Two overlapping 1 m apart aligned stratigraphically. Depths
#                 relative to the B core, which is why the top is not at 1270
#                 cm. Depths adjusted for post-coring shrinkage and for
#                 compression during coring. Compression determined by
#                 stratigraphic comparison.
#
